<p>The <b>2005 FIFA World Youth Championship</b> took place in the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> between 10 June and 2 July 2005. The 2005 championship was the 15th contested.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualification">Qualification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2005_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Qualification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The following 24 teams qualified for the 2005 FIFA World Youth Championship. Host country the Netherlands did not have to qualify for the tournament.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Squads">Squads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2005_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Squads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>For a list of all squads that played in the final tournament, see <i><a href="/wiki/2005_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship_squads" title="2005 FIFA World Youth Championship squads">2005 FIFA World Youth Championship squads</a></i>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_stages">Group stages</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2005_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Group stages">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The 24 teams were split into six groups of four teams. Six group winners, six second-place finishers and the four best third-place finishers qualify for the <a href="/wiki/Single-elimination_tournament#Creating_the_playoff_bracket_with_16_teams_advanced_from_6_groups_at_some_football_tournaments" title="Single-elimination tournament">knockout round</a>.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Round_of_16">Round of 16</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2005_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Round of 16">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="vevent" style="width: 100%; background-color: transparent; clear:both">
